38 #define LEVEL_OFF (-1)
39 #define LEVEL_ERROR (0)
40 #define LEVEL_WARN (1)
41 #define LEVEL_INFO (2)
42 #define LEVEL_TRACE (3)
43 #define LEVEL_NUM (4)
44 #define LEVEL_CRITICAL (5) /*LEVEL_CRITICAL log will be output as LEVEL_INFO, and it is NOT filtered by trace mask*/
45 
47 /*
48  * DBG_LEVEL is used to control the log printed by DBG_BUFFER(), DBG_INDEX() and DBG_TEXT().
49  * LEVEL_OFF : Print None
50  * LEVEL_ERROR : Print ERROR
51  * LEVEL_WARN : Print ERROR, WARN
52  * LEVEL_INFO : Print ERROR, WARN, INFO
53  * LEVEL_TRACE : Print ERROR, WARN, INFO, TRACE
54  */
55 #define DBG_LEVEL LEVEL_TRACE

314 #define COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, subtype, module, level) (uint32_t)(((type)<<24) | ((subtype)<<16) | ((module)<<8) | (level))
315 
316 /* Internal macro that is wrapped by internal macro DBG_BUFFER. */
317 #define DBG_BUFFER_INTERNAL(type, sub_type, module, level, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
318  static const char format[] TRACE_DATA = fmt;\
319  log_buffer(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, level), (uint32_t)format, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
320  } while (0)
321 
322 #if (DBG_LEVEL >= LEVEL_ERROR)
323 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_ERROR(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
324  DBG_BUFFER_INTERNAL(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_ERROR, fmt, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
325  } while (0)
326 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_ERROR(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
327  log_index(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_ERROR), fmt, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
328  } while (0)
329 #define DBG_TEXT_LEVEL_ERROR(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...) do {\
330  log_text(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_ERROR), fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
331  } while (0)
332 #else
333 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_ERROR(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...)
334 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_ERROR(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...)
335 #define DBG_TEXT_LEVEL_ERROR(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...)
336 #endif
337 
338 #if (DBG_LEVEL >= LEVEL_WARN)
339 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_WARN(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
340  DBG_BUFFER_INTERNAL(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_WARN, fmt, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
341  } while (0)
342 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_WARN(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
343  log_index(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_WARN), fmt, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
344  } while (0)
345 #define DBG_TEXT_LEVEL_WARN(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...) do {\
346  log_text(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_WARN), fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
347  } while (0)
348 #else
349 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_WARN(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...)
350 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_WARN(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...)
351 #define DBG_TEXT_LEVEL_WARN(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...)
352 #endif
353 
354 #if (DBG_LEVEL >= LEVEL_INFO)
355 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_INFO(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
356  DBG_BUFFER_INTERNAL(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_INFO, fmt, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
357  } while (0)
358 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_INFO(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\
359  log_index(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_INFO), fmt, param_num, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
360  } while (0)
361 #define DBG_TEXT_LEVEL_INFO(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...) do {\
362  log_text(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_INFO), fmt, ##__VA_ARGS__);\
363  } while (0)

366 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_CRITICAL(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...) do {\
367  DBG_BUFFER_INTERNAL(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_CRITICAL, fmt, COUNT_ARG(__VA_ARGS__), ##__VA_ARGS__);\
368  } while (0)
369 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_CRITICAL(type, sub_type, module, fmt, ...) do {\
370  log_index(COMBINE_TRACE_INFO(type, sub_type, module, LEVEL_CRITICAL), fmt, COUNT_ARG(__VA_ARGS__), ##__VA_ARGS__);\
371  } while (0)
372 #else
373 #define DBG_BUFFER_LEVEL_INFO(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...)

380 #if (DBG_LEVEL >= LEVEL_TRACE)

383  } while (0)
384 #define DBG_INDEX_LEVEL_TRACE(type, sub_type, module, fmt, param_num, ...) do {\

674 /* Patch Trace Interfaces */
675 #define PATCH_PRINT_ERROR0(fmt) \
676  DBG_INDEX(LOG_TYPE, SUBTYPE_INDEX, MODULE_PATCH, LEVEL_ERROR, fmt, 0)
677 #define PATCH_PRINT_ERROR1(fmt, arg0) \
678  DBG_INDEX(LOG_TYPE, SUBTYPE_INDEX, MODULE_PATCH, LEVEL_ERROR, fmt, 1, arg0)
679 #define PATCH_PRINT_ERROR2(fmt, arg0, arg1) \
680  DBG_INDEX(LOG_TYPE, SUBTYPE_INDEX, MODULE_PATCH, LEVEL_ERROR, fmt, 2, arg0, arg1)
681 #define PATCH_PRINT_ERROR3(fmt, arg0, arg1, arg2) \
682  DBG_INDEX(LOG_TYPE, SUBTYPE_INDEX, MODULE_PATCH, LEVEL_ERROR, fmt, 3, arg0, arg1, arg2)
683 #define PATCH_PRINT_ERROR4(fmt, arg0, arg1, arg2, arg3) \
684  DBG_INDEX(LOG_TYPE, SUBTYPE_INDEX, MODULE_PATCH, LEVEL_ERROR, fmt, 4, arg0, arg1, arg2, arg3)
685 #define PATCH_PRINT_ERROR5(fmt, arg0, arg1, arg2, arg3, arg4) \
